SELECT [t].[ClaimId], [c0].[Name] AS [CustomerName], [c0].[Phone], [p].[SerialNo], [p0].[Name] AS [ProductName], [t].[Status], [t].[ClaimDate], CASE
    WHEN [t].[AssignedTo] IS NULL THEN NULL
